		<script type="text/javascript">
			function hbTab(n) {
				for (var i = 1; i <= 2; i++) {
					if (i == n) {
						getObject("hbTab" + i).className = "ad_Tabopen";
						getObject("hbTable" + i).style.display = "";
					} else {
						getObject("hbTab" + i).className = "ad_Tabclose";
						getObject("hbTable" + i).style.display = "none";
					}
				}
			}

 <script type="text/javascript">
                var dhsubmit = false;
                var remQuery = "";
				var cursorPos = 0;
                
					getObject("searchform").query.value = manulQuery;
					//getObject("searchform").onblur();
                function erase(q) {
                    if (q.value == defaultQuery || q.value == manulQuery)q.value = '';
                    q.style.color = '#000';
                }
                function recovery(q) {
                    if (q.value == '') {
                        sf = getObject("searchform");
                        if (sf.action == "https://www.sogou.com/sohu")q.value = manulQuery;
                        else q.value = defaultQuery;
                        q.style.color = '#666';
                    }
                }
                function checkKw() {
                    var sf = getObject("searchform");
                    getObject("ast").value = parseInt(new Date().getTime() / 1000);
                    if (dhsubmit) {
                        dhsubmit = false;
                        return true;
                    }
                    if (globalsearchformaction != "") {
                        document.searchform.action = globalsearchformaction;
                    }
                    if (sf.action == "https://www.sogou.com/sohu") {
                        if (sf.query.value == manulQuery) {
                            sf.p.value = "01030140";
                            <!-- add ibm link -->
                            //window.open('http://goto.sogou.com/200902/c766b99502e6f8a6bc6fa312db6e1716.php');
                        }
                        else sf.p.value = "01040100";
                    }

                    var query = sf.query.value;
                    var URL;
                    if (sf.action == "http://map.sogou.com/new") {
                        if (query && query != defaultQuery) {
                            URL = sf.action + "/#lq=" + query;
                        } else {
                            URL = "http://map.sogou.com/";
                        }
                        window.open(URL);
                        return false;
                    }
                    if (query && query == defaultQuery) {
                        if (sf.action == "http://bbs.sogou.com/t")    sf.action = "http://bbs.sogou.com/";
                        if (sf.action == "http://mp3.sogou.com/music.so") sf.action = "http://mp3.sogou.com/sogou_phb/html/index.html";
                    }
                    if (query && query != defaultQuery) {
                        if (sf.action == "http://bbs.sogou.com/") sf.action = "http://bbs.sogou.com/t";
                        if (sf.action == "http://mp3.sogou.com/sogou_phb/html/index.html") sf.action = "http://mp3.sogou.com/music.so";
                    }
                    return true;
                }

                            sug$('suggimg2').onmouseover = function () {
                                nothide = true;
                            }
                            sug$('suggimg2').onmouseout = function () {
                                nothide = false;
                            }
                        }

                        var oldsub = $sForm.onsubmit;
                        $sForm.onsubmit = function (a, b, c) {
                            if (typeof oldsub == 'function')
                                oldsub(a, b, c);
                            if (globalsearchformaction != "")
                                $sForm.action = globalsearchformaction;
                            if ($sForm.action == "http://map.sogou.com/new")
                                return false;
                            if (cline == 0) {
                                var retUrl = clickWeb(sug$("keyword0"));
                                if (retUrl != "") {
                                    globalsearchformaction = $sForm.action;
                                    $sForm.action = REDIRECTPATH;
                                    $sForm.rturl.value = "http://" + retUrl.toLowerCase();
                                    cline = -1;
                                } else {
                                    pingBack("sb");
                                }
                            } else {
                                pingBack("sb");
                            }
                            hh.onblur();
                            return true;
                        }
                        //if (auto) getContent(sug$(inputid).value, false);
                    } else {
                        window.setTimeout(function () {
                            ali(auto)
                        }, 10);
                    }
                }

                this.ali = ali;

//create suggestion-s div
                function csd() {
                    indn = true;
                    var oR = document.createElement('div');
                    oR.id = 'sugmaindivname';
                    oR.style.zIndex = "2001";
                    oR.style.paddingRight = "0px";
                    oR.style.paddingLeft = "0px";
                    oR.style.paddingTop = "0px";
                    oR.style.paddingBottom = "0px";
                    oR.style.display = "none";
                    da(oR);
                    oR.style.position = "absolute";
                    oR.style.backgroundColor = "white";
                    document.body.appendChild(oR);
                    if (needIfm) {
                        var oFrame = document.createElement("IFRAME");
                        var oParentDIV = document.createElement("div");
                        oFrame.id = 'inthefrontIFRAME';
                        oFrame.setAttribute("frameBorder", "0");
                        oFrame.style.width = "2222px";
                        oFrame.style.height = "2222px";
                        oFrame.style.border = "0";

                        oParentDIV.id = 'inthefront';
                        oParentDIV.appendChild(oFrame);
                        oParentDIV.style.zIndex = "2000";
                        oParentDIV.style.paddingRight = "0";
                        oParentDIV.style.paddingLeft = "0";
                        oParentDIV.style.paddingTop = "0";
                        oParentDIV.style.paddingBottom = "0";
                        oParentDIV.style.display = "none";
                        oParentDIV.style.width = "10px";
                        oParentDIV.style.height = "10px";
                        oParentDIV.style.overflow = "hidden";
                        da(oParentDIV);
                        oParentDIV.style.position = "absolute";
                        document.body.appendChild(oParentDIV);
                    }
                    kbd();
                }

                function da(obj) {
                    if (obj) {
                        var inp = sug$(inputid);
                        var off = kb(inp);
                        var left = off[0];
                        var top = (off[1] + inp.offsetHeight);
                        if (sugLeft <= 0) {
                            left += sugLeft;
                            top += sugTop;
                        }
                        if (isIe) {
                            if (sugLeft <= 0)
                                left += 1;
                        }
                        obj.style.left = left + "px";
                        obj.style.top = top + "px";

                        if (sugWidth)
                            obj.style.width = sugWidth + "px";
                        else
                            obj.style.width = inp.offsetWidth + "px";
                    }
                }

//hide suggestion-s div
                function Wb() {
                    var hh = sug$('sugmaindivname');
                    if (hh && hh.style) {
                        hh.style.display = "none";
                        if (sug$('suggimg2'))
                            sug$('suggimg2').src = sug$('suggimg2').src.replace('up', 'down');
                        if (needIfm) {
                            sug$('inthefront').style.display = "none";
                        }
                    }
                }

//show hide suggestion-s div
                function onoff(th) {
                    th = th || sug$('suggimg2');
                    var hh = sug$('sugmaindivname');

                    if (hh && hh.style) {
                        if (th && th.src.indexOf('down.gif') > 0) {
                            sug$(inputid).focus();
                            getContent(sug$(inputid).value, true);
                        } else {
                            Wb();
                        }
                    }
                }

                this.onoff = onoff;

//key bind
                function kbd() {
                    var bt = new Date().getTime();
                    var keywordrand = Math.floor((Math.random()) * 10000);
                    var et = new Date().getTime();
                    if ((et - bt) < 500) {
                        var hh = sug$(inputid);
                        if (hh.addEventListener) {
                            hh.addEventListener('keydown', onlyNum, false);
                            hh.addEventListener('keyup', press, false);
                        } else if (hh.attachEvent) {
                            hh.attachEvent('onkeydown', onlyNum);
                            hh.attachEvent('onkeyup', press);
                        } else {
                            hh.onkeydown = onlyNum;
                            hh.onkeyup = press;
                        }
                    }
                }

//if ( !window.XMLHttpRequest )
                //XMLHttpRequest = function(){return new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP")};

                function handlelines(ls, ll, keywords, rr) {
                    var datas = ls.substring(1, ls.indexOf(']'));
                    if (datas)
                        datas = datas.split(", ");
                    else
                        datas = [];

                    var hh = "";
                    var hasWeb = false;

                    for (var i = 0; i < datas.length; i++) {
                        var nw = datas[i].split(";;");
                        if (nw.length < 2)
                            continue;

                        if (nw[1]) {
                            //mark red
                            var skey;
                            var curl;
                            var show;
                            var attInfo;


                            //isWeb
                            var isWeb = false;
                            var web = nw[0].split("|");
                            if (web.length > 1) {
                                isWeb = true;
                                hasWeb = true;
                                show = web[0];
                                attInfo = web[1];
                                skey = web[0];
                                curl = REDIRECTPATH + "?rturl=" + escape("http://" + attInfo);
                            } else {
                                show = nw[0];
                                skey = nw[0].replace(/'/g, "\\'");
                                curl = "https://www.sogou.com/sohu?query=" + escape(show) + "&p=" + $sForm.pid.value + "&w=" + suggestRid + "&_asf=www.sohu.com";
                            }

                            if (isWeb) {
                                show = "<em>" + show + "</em>";
                                show += "<br>";
                                show += "<span>http://" + attInfo + "</span><font color=#636363> - 推广</font>";
                            }
                            show = show + preFix;
                            if (nw[2] && nw[2] != nw[0]) {
                                show = show + "(" + nw[2] + preFix + ")";
                                skey = nw[2].replace(/'/g, "\\'");
                            }
                            hh += "<a href='" + curl + "' target=\"_blank\" onclick=\"sugCls.cc('" + ll + "',this)\">";
                            hh += "<li id=\"keyword" + ll + "\"  onmouseover='sugCls.ovo(" + ll + ")' onmouseout='sugCls.ovo(-1)'";
                            if (isWeb)
                                hh += " web = '" + attInfo + "'";
                            hh += " keys='" + skey + "'>";

                            //if(ll==0&&isWeb)
                            //hh += "<span class=\"menutip-s\">Ctrl+Enter打开网址</span>";
                            hh += "" + show + "</li></a>";
                        }
                        ll++;
                    }
                    return [hh, ll, hasWeb];
                }

                function handleContent(ee) {
                    ee = decodeURIComponent(ee.replace(/\+/g, " "));
                    oldresult = ee;
                    var ret = ee.split(';;&;;');
                    var hh;
                    var keywords = "";
                    cline = -1;
                    tlines = 0;
                    var hasWeb;

                    hh = '<div id="sugmaindivname2"  class="suggestion-s">';

                    if ((ret.length != 3)) {
                        hh += '<div class="menuintro-s">输入查询词即在此显示智能提示</div>';
                    } else {
                        keywords = ret[0].substring(ret[0].indexOf('[') + 1, ret[0].lastIndexOf(']'));
                        if (keywords)
                            keywords = keywords.split(", ");
                        else
                            keywords = [];

                        hh += '<ul class="menuitem-s">';
                        var si = 1;
                        if (revsd > 1) si = 2;
                        var reth = handlelines(ret[si], 0, keywords, si);
                        hh += reth[0];
                        hasWeb = reth[2];

                        reth = handlelines(ret[3 - si], reth[1], keywords, 3 - si);
                        hh += reth[0];
                        tlines = reth[1];

                        hh += '</ul>';
                        hh = hh.replace(/undefined/g, "");

                    }
                    hh += '<div class="menuswitch-s"><a onclick="sugCls.disableSug()" onmousedown="sugCls.reCursorPos()" class="menuoff-s">关闭</a>搜狗智能提示</div>';
                    hh += '</div>';
                    if (sug$("sugmaindivname")) {
                        sug$("sugmaindivname").innerHTML = hh;
                        if (tlines == 0 && keywords.length > 0)
                            Wb();
                        else {
                            if (sug$("sugmaindivname").style.display == "none")
                                pingBack("show_s");
                            sug$("sugmaindivname").style.display = "block";

                            if (sug$('suggimg2'))
                                sug$('suggimg2').src = sug$('suggimg2').src.replace('down', 'up');
                            if (needIfm) {
                                sug$('inthefront').style.height = iframeHeight + "px";
                                sug$('inthefront').style.display = "block";
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                this.handleContent = handleContent;

                this.revs = function (th) {
                    if (revsd == 1)
                        revsd = 2;
                    else
                        revsd = 1;
                    handleContent(oldresult);
                }

                function getContent(keyword, showspace) {
                    //if !web return
                    if (globalsearchformaction.indexOf("www.sogou.com") == -1)
                        return;

                    if ($sForm.w)
                        $sForm.w.value = normalRid || 0;
                    if (SugPara['enableSug'] && enableSug) {
                        if ((!showspace) && (keyword == "")) {
                            Wb();
                            SugPara['isSug'] = false;
                            return;
                        }

                        if (oqy.replace(/\s/g, "").replace(/ /g, "") && (oqy == keyword)) {
                            if (oldresult)
                                handleContent(oldresult);
                            return;
                        }
                        SugPara['isSug'] = false;

                        oqy = keyword;
                        if (xmlhttp1) {
                            try {
                                xmlhttp1.destroy();
                            } catch (e) {
                            }
                            xmlhttp1 = null;
                        }

                        var newStrComment = encodeURIComponent(keyword);
                        var domain = SugPara['domain'] || "w.sugg.sogou.com";
                        var url = "http://" + domain + "/sugg/suggestajaj.jsp?key=" + newStrComment + "&type=" + sugType + "&pr=" + (SugPara['productId'] || sugType);
                        var tt = new Date().getTime();
                        if (newStrComment.replace(/\s/g, "").replace(/ /g, "") == "")
                            url += "&rd=" + tt;

                        xmlhttp1 = new sAjaj(url);

                    } else {
                        SugPara['isSug'] = false;
                        Wb();
                        oqy = "uaofwequroasjdklf";
                    }
                }

                this.getContent = getContent;

//click one
                function cc(ss, aobj) {
                    aobj.href += "&_ast=" + Math.round(new Date().getTime() / 1000);
                    document.oncontextmenu = sdf;
                    var hh = sug$(inputid);
                    var tmp = "";
                    var cobj = sug$("keyword" + ss);

                    if (cobj)
                        tmp = cobj.getAttribute("keys").toLowerCase();
                    hh.value = tmp;
                    Wb();
                    hh.focus();

                    SugPara['isSug'] = true;
                    if (clickWeb(cobj) == "")
                        pingBack('sb');
                    SugPara['isSug'] = false;

                }

                this.cc = cc;

                function clickWeb(cobj) {
                    var web = "";
                    if (cobj)
                        web = cobj.getAttribute("web");
                    if (web) {
                        cline = 0;
                        pingBack("c_nav");
                        return web;
                    }
                    return "";
                }

                function kb(s) {
                    var x = 0;
                    var y = 0;
                    while (s) {
                        x += s.offsetLeft;
                        y += s.offsetTop;
                        s = s.offsetParent;
                    }
                    return [x, y];
                }

                this.ovo = function (cur) {
                    cline = cur;
                    for (var i = 0; i < tlines; i++) {
                        if (i == cur) {
                            sug$("keyword" + i).style.background = "#F1F1F1";
                        } else {
                            sug$("keyword" + i).style.background = "#ffffff";
                        }
                    }
                }

                function sdf(ev) {
                    ev = ev || window.event;
                    if (ev.preventDefault)
                        ev.preventDefault();
                    else
                        ev.returnValue = false;
                    if (ev.stopPropagation)
                        ev.stopPropagation();
                    else
                        ev.cancelBubble = true;
                }

                var bak;

                function press(ev) {

                    if (!SugPara['enableSug']) return;

                    ev = ev || window.event;
                    sdf(ev);
                    if ((ev.keyCode == 9) || (ev.keyCode == 38) || (ev.keyCode == 40))
                        return false;
                    else
                        bak = sug$(inputid).value;

                    if (ev.keyCode == 13 && submited) {
                        submited = false;
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (sug$(inputid).value == "")
                        enableSug = true;

                    getContent(sug$(inputid).value, false);
                }

                function onlyNum(ev) {
                    ev = ev || window.event;

                    if (ev.keyCode == 13) {
                        submited = true;
                        return;
                    }

                    if (!SugPara['enableSug']) return;
                    if (!enableSug) return;
                    if (!sug$("sugmaindivname"))return;
                    if (sug$("sugmaindivname").style.display == 'none')
                        return;

                    var tmp;
                    var clineObj;
                    if (ev.keyCode == 40 || ev.keyCode == 9) // key = down or key = tab
                    {
                        sdf(ev);
                        if (cline < tlines - 1) {
                            cline++;
                        } else if (cline == tlines - 1) {
                            cline = tlines;
                        } else {
                            cline = 0;
                        }

                    }
                    else if (ev.keyCode == 38)   //key= up
                    {
                        sdf(ev);
                        if (cline == -1)
                            cline = tlines;
                        if (cline >= 0) {
                            cline--;
                        }

                    }
                    if (ev.keyCode == 40 || ev.keyCode == 9 || ev.keyCode == 38) {
                        that.ovo(cline);
                        clineObj = sug$("keyword" + cline);
                        if (clineObj)
                            tmp = clineObj.getAttribute("keys").toLowerCase();
                        else
                            tmp = bak;
                        sug$(inputid).value = tmp;

                        if (cline == tlines || cline == -1) {
                            $sForm.w.value = normalRid || 0;
                            SugPara['isSug'] = false;
                        } else if ($sForm.w) {
                            $sForm.w.value = suggestRid || 0;
                            SugPara['isSug'] = true;
                        }
                        return false;
                    }
                }

                var sugPings = new Array(); //ping back
                function pingBack(act) {
                    if (globalsearchformaction.indexOf("www.sogou.com") == -1)
                        return;
                    var s1 = "http://61.135.188.217:8080/c.jpg";
                    var s2 = "http://pb.sogou.com/sugg.gif";
                    var url = "?w=" + encodeURIComponent(sug$(inputid).value) + "&k=" + bak + "&type=" + sugType + "&s=";
                    if (SugPara['isSug'])
                        url += "t";
                    else
                        url += "f";

                    if (cline != -1)
                        url += "&cline=" + cline;
                    if (act)
                        url += "&act=" + act;
                    url += "&r=" + new Date().getSeconds();

                    var V = sugPings.length;
                    sugPings[V + 1] = new Image();
                    sugPings[V + 1].src = s2 + url;

                }

//disable sug
                function disableSug() {
                    Wb();
					setCaretPosition(document.getElementById('query'),cursorPos);
                    enableSug = false;
                    pingBack("dis");
                    return false;
                }

                this.disableSug = disableSug;
				function reCursorPos(){
					cursorPos = getCursortPosition(document.getElementById('query'));
				}
				this.reCursorPos = reCursorPos;
                function sug$(objName) {
                    if (document.getElementById)
                        return document.getElementById(objName);
                    else
                        return document.all[objName];
                }
				//
				function getCursortPosition(ctrl) {
					var CaretPos = 0;
					// IE Support
					if (document.selection) {
						ctrl.focus();
						var Sel = document.selection.createRange();
						Sel.moveStart('character', -ctrl.value.length);
						CaretPos = Sel.text.length;

					}
					// Firefox support
					else if (ctrl.selectionStart || ctrl.selectionStart == '0')
					CaretPos = ctrl.selectionStart;
					return (CaretPos);
				}
				//
				function setCaretPosition(ctrl, pos){
					if(ctrl.setSelectionRange)
					{
						ctrl.focus();
						ctrl.setSelectionRange(pos,pos);
					}
					else if (ctrl.createTextRange) {
						var range = ctrl.createTextRange();
						range.collapse(true);
						range.moveEnd('character', pos);
						range.moveStart('character', pos);
						range.select();
					}
				}
            }();
            $sForm.query.onkeydown = sugCls.ali;
            var onoff = sugCls.onoff;
            </script>

<h1 collection="Y"><span class="iconB"></span><span><a href="http://media.sohu.com/" target="_blank">搜狐视角</a></span><a class="sohu-pic" href="http://news.sohu.com/photo/" target="_blank">搜狐图片</a></h1>
						<div id="pic-roll">
<div id="pic-wrap">
<div id="pic-cont">
<ul> 

<li><a href="http://pic.news.sohu.com/group-685086.shtml" target="_blank"><img src="http://i2.itc.cn/20150921/3616_4cb0f249_b7ea_ba67_ddd7_a6a9d845e6f6_1.jpg"></a><span><i></i><a href="http://pic.news.sohu.com/group-685086.shtml" target="_blank">熊猫盼盼开“百岁”party</a></span></li>


<li><a href="http://pic.news.sohu.com/group-685043.shtml" target="_blank"><img src="http://i0.itc.cn/20150921/3616_3f6250a6_a67d_eb5d_f3f3_e74c7b69f034_1.jpg"></a><span><i></i><a href="http://pic.news.sohu.com/group-685043.shtml" target="_blank">李克强拧螺丝的非洲轻轨通车</a></span></li>

<li><a href="http://pic.news.sohu.com/group-684945.shtml" target="_blank"><img src="http://i0.itc.cn/20150921/3616_509abed7_7ee2_0c31_fe53_fd5438c1862c_1.jpg"></a><span><i></i><a href="http://pic.news.sohu.com/group-684945.shtml" target="_blank">13岁难民盾牌阵前拉小提琴</a></span></li>



<li><a href="http://pic.news.sohu.com/group-684888.shtml" target="_blank"><img src="http://i3.itc.cn/20150921/3616_cc732241_1fe7_fafd_0d18_abaf8986b2e7_1.jpg"></a><span><i></i><a href="http://pic.news.sohu.com/group-684888.shtml" target="_blank">被绊倒难民男孩牵手C罗入球场</a></span></li>

<script type="text/javascript">
	(function(){

		var startPic = getStartPos(),
			startOK = false;
		function getStartPos(){
			var hash = document.location.hash;
				hash = hash.substring(1);
			if(/img\d{1}/g.test(hash)){
				return /img(\d)/g.exec(hash)[1];
				//return hash.substring(3,4);
			}
		}
		function picRolling(){	
			var getUl=document.getElementById('pic-cont'),getLi=getUl.getElementsByTagName('li'),getImg=getUl.getElementsByTagName('img'),	
			getRight=document.getElementById('right-btn'),getLeft=document.getElementById('left-btn'),	
			timer=null, //连续滚动的计时器	
			timer_one = null, //滚动一张图的计时器	
			shifting = 10, //滚动单位,一次滚动多少	
			speed = 5, //循环滚动的小时间间隔	
			timer_out = null, //滚动过程中的停顿	
			ifMouseOver = false, //标志位,鼠标是否悬停	
			imgWidth = 190, //图片宽度	
			temp = 0,	
			newUlNode = document.createElement('ul'); //为让图片能无缝滚动,在这组图片后面再复制一组图片;	
			getUl.appendChild(newUlNode);	
			newUlNode.innerHTML = getUl.getElementsByTagName('ul')[0].innerHTML;	
			getUl.style.width = (getLi[0].offsetWidth)*getLi.length+'px'; //设置可显示的宽度范围	
			var ulWidth = getUl.offsetWidth;	
			if(startPic){
				var leftPicPos = -imgWidth*(startPic-1);
				getUl.style.left = leftPicPos+'px';
				temp = leftPicPos;
				setTimeout(function(){startOK = true},15000);
			}else{
				startOK = true;
			}
			timer_out = window.setTimeout(function(){timer=setInterval(roll,speed)},3000);	
			getRight.onclick=function(){ //点右按钮后,滚动一张图片	
				if(temp % imgWidth == 0){ //保证滚动完一整张图,也就是在只滚动了半张图的情况下,不触发按钮	
					theShifting = 0 - shifting;	
					clearInterval(timer);	
					clearTimeout(timer_out);	
					timer_one = setInterval(rollOneTime,speed);	
				}		
				return false;	
			}	
			getRight.onmouseover = function(){	
				getRight.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "now-btn";	
				getLeft.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "now-btn";	
			}	
			getLeft.onmouseover = function(){	
				getRight.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "now-btn";	
				getLeft.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "now-btn";	
			}	
			getRight.onmouseout = function(){	
				getRight.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "";	
				getLeft.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "";	
			}	
			getLeft.onmouseout = function(){	
				getRight.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "";	
				getLeft.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "";	
			}	
			getLeft.onclick=function(){ //点左按钮后,滚动一张图片	
				if(temp % imgWidth == 0){ //保证滚动完一整张图,也就是在只滚动了半张图的情况下,不触发按钮	
					theShifting = shifting;	
					clearInterval(timer);	
					clearTimeout(timer_out);	
					timer_one = setInterval(rollOneTime,speed);	
				}		
				return false;	
			}
			function rollOneTime(){  //组图只滚动一张图片的距离,也就是只滚动一张图片	
				clearInterval(timer);	
				clearTimeout(timer_out);	
				getUl.style.left = temp + theShifting + 'px';  //每次挪动theShifting个像素,temp记录了offsetLeft值	
				temp = temp + theShifting; //temp记录了offsetLeft值	
				if(temp % imgWidth == 0){ //保证滚动完一整张图	
					clearInterval(timer_one);	
					clearInterval(timer);	
					timer_out = window.setTimeout(function(){timer=setInterval(roll,speed)},3000); //保证图展示3秒后在执行roll	
				}
				if(temp < -ulWidth/2){ //temp记录了offsetLeft值,当整组图向左都挪动完时,组图重新定位left值为0	
					getUl.style.left=0;	
					temp = 0;	
				}	
				if(temp > 0){ //当整组图向右都挪动完时,组图重新定位left值	
					getUl.style.left = -ulWidth/2+'px';	
					temp = -ulWidth/2;	
				}		
			}	
			function roll(){  //组图循环滚动	
				if(!startOK){return};
				clearInterval(timer_one);	
				clearTimeout(timer_out);	
				theShifting = 0 - shifting;  //默认组图向左滚动	
				getUl.style.left = temp + theShifting+'px'; //每次挪动theShifting个像素,temp记录了offsetLeft值	
				temp = temp + theShifting;  //temp记录了offsetLeft值	
				if(temp % imgWidth == 0){ //保证滚动完一整张图	
					clearInterval(timer);	
					if(!ifMouseOver){	
						timer_out = window.setTimeout(function(){timer=setInterval(roll,speed)},3000); //保证图展示3秒后在执行roll	
					}	
				}	
				if(temp<-ulWidth/2){  //temp记录了offsetLeft值,当整组图向左都挪动完时,组图重新定位left值为0	
					getUl.style.left=0;	
					temp = 0;	
				}	
				if(temp>0){ //当整组图向右都挪动完时,组图重新定位left值	
					getUl.style.left=-ulWidth/2+'px';	
					temp = -ulWidth/2;	
				}	
			}									
			for(var i=0; i<getLi.length; i++){   //遍历每张图,在每张图上绑定mouseover,mouseout事件	
				getLi[i].onmouseover=function(){ //鼠标悬停在图片上时取消滚动	
					if(getUl.offsetLeft % imgWidth == 0){  //保证滚动完一整张图再取消滚动,避免出现停留在半张图状态	
						clearInterval(timer);	
						clearTimeout(timer_out);	
						getRight.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "now-btn";	
						getLeft.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "now-btn";	
					}	
				}	
				getLi[i].onmouseout=function(){ //鼠标挪出图片继续滚动	
					if(getUl.offsetLeft % imgWidth == 0){	
						clearInterval(timer);	
						clearTimeout(timer_out);	
						getRight.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "";	
						getLeft.getElementsByTagName("a")[0].className = "";	
						timer_out = window.setTimeout(function(){timer=setInterval(roll,speed)},3000);	
					}	
				}	
			}	
		}	
		//window.onload = function(){picRolling();}	
		if(window.attachEvent){	
			window.attachEvent("onload", picRolling);	
		}else{	
			window.addEventListener("load", picRolling , false);	
		}	
	})()	
</script>

                                               var carBm = {
                                                        'bid' : 'brand',
                                                        'mid' : 'model',
                                                        'pb' : 'select-brand',
                                                        'mb' : 'select-model',

                                               };
                                               
                                               
                                               carBm.init = function(){
                                                        this.getBmData();
                                                        this.setBind();
                                               }
                                               
                                               
                                               carBm.setBind = function(){
                                               
                                                        var bEL = _$('brand'),
                                                                 mEL = _$('model'),

                                                                 self.clearChild();

                                                                 self.setPselect(elem);
                                                                 self.getChild(mid);
                                                                 self.setText(mbEL,'请选择');
                                                                 _$(self.mhid).value = 0;
                                                                 return false;
                                                        });
                                                        
                                                        this.bind(mEL, 'click', function(e){
                                                                 var elem = e.target || e.srcElement;
                                                                 var childElem = elem.childNodes;
                                                                 
                                                                 if(elem.nodeName == 'STRONG' || childElem[0].nodeName == 'STRONG'){
                                                                           return false;
                                                                 }
                                                                 var pElem = elem.parentNode;
                                                                 var mid = pElem.getAttribute('data-id');
                                                                 self.setText(_$(self.mb),elem.innerHTML.toString())
                                                                 self.setMselect(mid);
                                                                 carBm.close();
                                                                 return false;
                                                        });
                                                        
                                                        this.bind(pbEL, 'click', function(e){
                                                                 self.close();
                                                                 bEL.parentNode.style.display = '';
                                                                 return false;
                                                        });

                                                                           self.close();

                                                        });
                                               }
                                               
                                               
                                               carBm.doSearch = function(){
                                                        this.close();
                                                        
                                                        var _pval = _$(this.phid).value.toString(),
                                                                 _mval = _$(this.mhid).value.toString(),
                                                                 reditUrl = '';
                            
                                                        if(_pval == "0"){
                                                                 alert('请选择品牌');
                                                                 return false;
                                                        }

                                                                 reditUrl = this.searchUrl.replace('{KEYWORD}',escape(_pval));
                                                        }
                                                        
                                                        window.open(reditUrl);
                                                        return false;
                                               }
                                               
                                               carBm.setPselect = function(EL){

                                               carBm.getChild = function(mid){
                                                        
                                                        var i = 0,
                                                                 c = brandMods.length,
                                                                 data = brandMods,
                                                                 cnum = 0, //子类
                                                                 cdata = '';
                            
                                                        for(; i<c; i++){
                                                                 if(data[i].i == mid){
                                                                           cdata = data[i].s;
                                                                           _getChildOption(cdata);
                                                                           break;
                                                                 }
                                                        }
                                                        
                                                        function _getChildOption(cdata){
                                                                 if(!cdata) return false;
                                                                 
                                                                 var k = 0;
                                                                 cnum = data[i].s.length;
                                                                 
                                                                 for(; k<cnum; k++){
                                                                           var childData = cdata[k],
                                                                                    childDataCount = childData.b.length,
                                                                                    childList = cdata[k].b,         //子组数据
                                                                                    optionGroup = childData.n,//option 组名称
                                                                                    pOption = '',
                                                                                    cOption = ''; 
                                                                                    
                                                                           pOption = document.createElement("li");
                                                                           pOption.innerHTML = '<a href="javascript:;"><strong>'+optionGroup+'</strong></a>';
                                                                           _$('model').appendChild(pOption);
                            
                                                                           for(var n = 0; n < childDataCount; n++){
                                                                                    cOption = document.createElement("li");
                                                                                    cOption.setAttribute('data-id',childList[n].i);
                                                                                    cOption.innerHTML = '<a href="javascript:;">'+childList[n].n+'</a>';
                                                                                    _$('model').appendChild(cOption);
                                                                           }
                                                                           
                                                                 }
                                                        }
                                               }
                                               
                            
                                               carBm.clearChild = function(){

                                               carBm.getParent = function(bmData){
                                                        
                                                        var i = 0, 
                                                                 c = bmData.length,
                                                                 n = '', // name
                                                                 d = 0;        // id
                            
                                                        for( ; i<c; i++){
                                                                 var eli = document.createElement("li");

                                                                 d = bmData[i].i;
                                                                 eli.setAttribute('data-id',d);
                                                                 eli.innerHTML= '<a href="javascript:;">'+n+'</a>';
                                                                 _$("brand").appendChild(eli);
                                                        }
                                               }
                                               
                                               carBm.close = function(){

                                                        _$('model').parentNode.style.display = 'none';
                                               }
                                               
                                               carBm.bind = function(obj, type, fun){
                                               
                                                        function addEvent(obj, type, fun){
                                                                 if (obj.addEventListener) {
                                                                           obj.addEventListener(type, fun);
                                                                           return true;
                                                                 } else if (obj.attachEvent) {
                                                                           return obj.attachEvent("on" + type, fun);
                                                                 } else {
                                                                           return false;
                                                                 };
                                                        }
                                                        addEvent(obj, type, fun);
                                               }

                                                                             }
                                                                  };
                                                         }else {
                                                                   script.onload = function(){
                                                                                    func&&func(); 
                                                                   }
                                                         }  
                                                         script.src = js; 
                                                         document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);  
                                               }

function changeAutomn(n){
	if (n == 0) {
		$("sa-auto-tab").className = "titleB autotab_1";
		$("sa-autocontent1").className = "show";
		$("sa-autocontent2").className = "hidden";
		$("sa-autocontent3").className = "hidden";
	}else if(n == 1){
		$("sa-auto-tab").className = "titleB autotab_2";
		$("sa-autocontent1").className = "hidden";
		$("sa-autocontent2").className = "show";
		$("sa-autocontent3").className = "hidden";
	}else{
		$("sa-auto-tab").className = "titleB autotab_3";
		$("sa-autocontent1").className = "hidden";
		$("sa-autocontent2").className = "hidden";
		$("sa-autocontent3").className = "show";
	}
}

				curclass.className="div_c hand";

			function innerhtml(crand) {
